if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_11();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '945f0a7f510e108971afc705aa23fec2a387d9bf') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '945f0a7f510e108971afc705aa23fec2a387d9bf') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'e7475728de4f97590b0bcfddbed1f883baceb240') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '945f0a7f510e108971afc705aa23fec2a387d9bf') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('dev/test/test_database_plugins.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/test/test_database_plugins.php');
	writefile_12();
	if (!is_file('dev/test/test_database_plugins.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/test/test_database_plugins.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/test/test_database_plugins.php') != '5506842803670b50bf46cfe6198c0ea4dcd77a97') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/test/test_database_plugins.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/test/test_database_plugins.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/test/test_database_plugins.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/test/test_database_plugins.php') !== '5506842803670b50bf46cfe6198c0ea4dcd77a97') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/test/test_database_plugins.php') !== '65c10a4c9ccda7389348375d6c2705a19ff1515b') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/test/test_database_plugins.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/test/test_database_plugins.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/test/test_database_plugins.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/test/test_database_plugins.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_12();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/test/test_database_plugins.php') !== '5506842803670b50bf46cfe6198c0ea4dcd77a97') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/test/test_database_plugins.php');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', 0644)) {

	}

			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');

		writefile_13();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== 'a1fc28d6a31ff9ce661c0fac9d1f7865d1988f91') {

	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusDatabasePlugin.class.php') != 'b247eee965d774f08d1e4f49b4656c4f4cfb15d3') {

	}

	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusDatabasePlugin.class.php') !== 'b247eee965d774f08d1e4f49b4656c4f4cfb15d3') {

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplusDatabasePlugin.class.php');

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusDatabasePlugin.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_14();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusDatabasePlugin.class.php') !== 'b247eee965d774f08d1e4f49b4656c4f4cfb15d3') {

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio') != 'b42ba5355cf728cff192126315c013e9dc25aa18') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio') !== 'b42ba5355cf728cff192126315c013e9dc25aa18') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio') !== '2cdbc4c8648b4eccad8167bd2def7ca8f70dd69b') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_15();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio') !== 'b42ba5355cf728cff192126315c013e9dc25aa18') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.png')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/class_diagram.png');
	writefile_16();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.png')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/class_diagram.png');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.png') != '86d9e9eeb5d53796e9e737ffdc2c241de14f8c79') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/class_diagram.png');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/class_diagram.png', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/class_diagram.png');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.png') !== '86d9e9eeb5d53796e9e737ffdc2c241de14f8c79') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.png') !== '03170e23c7682f6f52b5d7c8b45a37abb571055c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/class_diagram.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/class_diagram.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/class_diagram.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/class_diagram.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_16();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.png') !== '86d9e9eeb5d53796e9e737ffdc2c241de14f8c79') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/class_diagram.png');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
	writefile_22();
	if (!is_file('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png') != '140a1429c12de9b9dad0ce8981587853bea0eeb1') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png') !== '140a1429c12de9b9dad0ce8981587853bea0eeb1') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png') !== 'e5951124e7a84fee421bfc3a61e72e7677187901') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_22();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png') !== '140a1429c12de9b9dad0ce8981587853bea0eeb1') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php') != 'ac2f9d79abd0b5b5304859914967ce7f46883ae7') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php') !== 'ac2f9d79abd0b5b5304859914967ce7f46883ae7') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php') !== '7f157f7abe8650aeec272a620107ef4c893a0b55') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_23();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php') !== 'ac2f9d79abd0b5b5304859914967ce7f46883ae7') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');

	writefile_24();
	if (!is_file('plugins/database/odbc/plugin.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/odbc/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/odbc/plugin.inc.php') != 'bf39a629c41662a387a12b1282b4821399a3aa07') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/odbc/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/odbc/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/database/odbc/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/odbc/plugin.inc.php') !== 'bf39a629c41662a387a12b1282b4821399a3aa07') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/odbc/plugin.inc.php') !== '946a790a1716b8a4dfc27c1db27bd1a48e431e9e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/database/odbc/plugin.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/database/odbc/plugin.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/database/odbc/plugin.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/database/odbc/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_24();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/odbc/plugin.inc.php') !== 'bf39a629c41662a387a12b1282b4821399a3aa07') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/odbc/plugin.inc.php');
		}
	}

if (!is_file('plugins/database/odbc/setup.part.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/database/odbc/setup.part.html');
	writefile_25();
	if (!is_file('plugins/database/odbc/setup.part.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/odbc/setup.part.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/odbc/setup.part.html') != 'dc04a7100d6b8542cee23da1862f58a192384316') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/odbc/setup.part.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/odbc/setup.part.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/database/odbc/setup.part.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/odbc/setup.part.html') !== 'dc04a7100d6b8542cee23da1862f58a192384316') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/odbc/setup.part.html') !== 'a2676637f76966fe8230033901b7d4ecc7ab1024') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/database/odbc/setup.part.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/database/odbc/setup.part.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/database/odbc/setup.part.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/database/odbc/setup.part.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_25();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/odbc/setup.part.html') !== 'dc04a7100d6b8542cee23da1862f58a192384316') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/odbc/setup.part.html');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/database/pdo/setup.part.html');
	writefile_26();
	if (!is_file('plugins/database/pdo/setup.part.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/pdo/setup.part.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/pdo/setup.part.html') != '36f5b34c2d982226a9056c606f2e5a45efdf1056') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/pdo/setup.part.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/pdo/setup.part.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/database/pdo/setup.part.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/pdo/setup.part.html') !== '36f5b34c2d982226a9056c606f2e5a45efdf1056') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/pdo/setup.part.html') !== 'd8b3600176ef042192325cca87ac11fedb6fcdfc') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/database/pdo/setup.part.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/database/pdo/setup.part.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/database/pdo/setup.part.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/database/pdo/setup.part.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_26();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/pdo/setup.part.html') !== '36f5b34c2d982226a9056c606f2e5a45efdf1056') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/pdo/setup.part.html');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/database/pgsql/plugin.inc.php');
	writefile_27();

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/pgsql/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/pgsql/plugin.inc.php') != 'a7cf48b68f1c3a7ff97fc0a062a5fbd112ade01f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/pgsql/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/pgsql/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/database/pgsql/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/pgsql/plugin.inc.php') !== 'a7cf48b68f1c3a7ff97fc0a062a5fbd112ade01f') {

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/database/pgsql/plugin.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/database/pgsql/plugin.inc.php');

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/database/pgsql/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_27();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/pgsql/plugin.inc.php') !== 'a7cf48b68f1c3a7ff97fc0a062a5fbd112ade01f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/pgsql/plugin.inc.php');

}

			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/struct_with_examples.sql.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/struct_with_examples.sql.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/struct_with_examples.sql.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_32();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/struct_with_examples.sql.php') !== 'b4ef698023fe5c20bb91a5b61e3ea7868ea483db') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/struct_with_examples.sql.php');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 274\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 274') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
